No. II(1)/AG/24/2017.—In exercise of the powers conferred by clause (a) of sub-section (1) of Section 9 of the
Tamil Nadu Agricultural Produce Marketing (Regulation) Act, 1987 (Tamil Nadu Act 27 of 1989), the Governor of
Tamil Nadu hereby excludes the areas specified in column (2) from the notified market areas specified in column (3)
of the Table below, so as to include the said areas into the proposed notified market area of Thirunavalur with effect
on and from the 09th day of June 2017:—

[¢Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 141, «õ÷£‡¬ñ («õM.2)ˆ ¶¬ø, 9 ü¨¡ 2017, ¬õè£C 26, «ýM÷‹H,

No. II(1)/AG/25/2017.—In exercise of the powers conferred  by sub-section (2) of  Section 6 of the Tamil Nadu
Agricultural Produce Marketing (Regulation) Act, 1987 (Tamil Nadu Act 27 of 1989), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby
declares the area of Thirunavalur Regulated Market under the Villupuram Market Committee specified in column (1) of
the Table below and the areas around the Thirunavalur Regulated Market comprising of the areas specified in the
corresponding entries in column (2) thereof, to be the notified market area of Thirunavalur Regulated Market for the purposes
of the said Act, in respect of all notified Agricultural Produces:-
